● iTa'awun Development Session Summary

  Vision Document Overview (from iTaawun_Documentation.docx)

  Product: iTa'awun (نواعتلا - Mutual Assistance) - A student-centric physical freelance hub platform for Malaysian university students.

  Core Concepts:
  - Live Gigs - P2P task board where Members post micro-tasks, Taskers fulfill them
  - Campus Vendors - Shopee-style storefront for student products/services
  - Tiered Roles - Member → Tasker (admin-approved) → Asnaf (income-verified, hidden flag)
  - Trust Architecture - Trust score, keyword filters, photo proof, audit logs
  - 0% Commission - P2P direct payment, platform takes no cut

  ---
  Gap Analysis Completed

  ---
  Changes Made This Session

  1. Database Schema Updates (schema-updates.sql)

  Created comprehensive SQL migration adding:

  New Tables:
  - gigs - Live Gig posts with status workflow
  - gig_claims - Tasker claims (one per gig)
  - gig_completions - Photo proof + requester confirmation
  - gig_flags - Community reports (auto-hide at 3)
  - verifications - Asnaf income doc verification
  - audit_logs - Immutable action trail for authorities
  - keyword_filters - Banned academic integrity keywords

  New Columns on profiles:
  - trust_score - Increments on completions
  - is_asnaf - Hidden flag (admin-only visible)
  - matric_card_url - Optional trust badge
  - income_doc_url - Asnaf verification doc

  New Columns on services:
  - flag_count - Community reports
  - auto_post - Trust privilege (≥3 completions)
  - expires_at - Auto-expire old gigs

  Functions & Triggers:
  - check_gig_integrity() - Regex keyword scanner
  - increment_trust_score() - Trust builder
  - check_gig_flags() - Auto-flag trigger @ 3 reports
  - log_audit() - Append-only audit logging

  ---

  Files to Create/Update:

  297     const SUPABASE_URL = 'https://fyahebgkacjsxmiwteny.supabase.co'
  298     const SUPABASE_KEY = 'eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9.eyJpc3MiOiJzdXBhYmFzZSIsInJlZiI6ImZ5YWhlYmdrYWNqc3htaXd0ZW55Iiwicm9s
      ZSI6ImFub24iLCJpYXQiOjE3NzAyNTg3NDEsImV4cCI6MjA4NTgzNDc0MX0.eIAWIPzB6EjW7rPKHLSsc2ryUBQ7yicRK1I-SxXg_2Y'
  299     const db = supabase.createClient(SUPABASE_URL, SUPABASE_KEY)
  300
  301     const BANNED_KEYWORDS = [
  302       'assignment', 'homework', 'exam', 'quiz', 'thesis', 'essay',
  303       'dissertation', 'paper', 'coursework', 'term paper', 'final project',
  304       'tugasan', 'ujian', 'tesis', 'karangan'
  305     ]
  306
  307     let currentUser = null
  308     let currentProfile = null
  309     let keywordDetected = false
  310
  311     // Auth check
  312     (async function init() {
  313       const { data: { session } } = await db.auth.getSession()
  314       if (!session) {
  315         window.location.href = 'index.html'
  316         return
  317       }
  318       currentUser = session.user
  319
  320       // Load profile
  321       const { data: profile } = await db.from('profiles').select('*').eq('id', currentUser.id).single()
  322       currentProfile = profile
  323
  324       if (profile?.avatar_url) {
  325         document.getElementById('profilePic').src = profile.avatar_url
  326       }
  327     })()
  328
  329     // Character count
  330     document.getElementById('description').addEventListener('input', function() {
  331       document.getElementById('charCount').textContent = this.value.length
  332     })
  333
  334     // Keyword detection
  335     function checkKeywords() {
  336       const title = document.getElementById('title').value.toLowerCase()
  337       const desc = document.getElementById('description').value.toLowerCase()
  338       const combined = title + ' ' + desc
  339
  340       keywordDetected = BANNED_KEYWORDS.some(keyword => {
  341         const regex = new RegExp('\\b' + keyword + '\\b', 'i')
  342         return regex.test(combined)
  343       })
  344
  345       const warning = document.getElementById('keywordWarning')
  346       warning.style.display = keywordDetected ? 'block' : 'none'
  347     }
  348
  349     // Form submission
  350     document.getElementById('gigForm').addEventListener('submit', async function(e) {
  351       e.preventDefault()
  352
  353       const title = document.getElementById('title').value.trim()
  354       const description = document.getElementById('description').value.trim()
  355       const reward = parseFloat(document.getElementById('reward').value)
  356       const location = document.getElementById('location').value.trim()
  357       const expires = document.getElementById('expires').value || null
  358
  359       if (!title || !description || !reward || !location) {
  360         showError('Please fill in all required fields.')
  361         return
  362       }
  363
  364       if (description.length > 500) {
  365         showError('Description must be 500 characters or less.')
  366         return
  367       }
  368
  369       const btn = document.getElementById('submitBtn')
  370       btn.disabled = true
  371       btn.textContent = 'Submitting...'
  372
  373       // Determine status based on trust score and keywords
  374       let status = 'pending_review'
  375       const trustScore = currentProfile?.trust_score || 0
  376       const hasAutoPost = currentProfile?.auto_post || false
  377
  378       // Auto-post if: trust score >= 3 AND no keywords detected
  379       if (trustScore >= 3 && !keywordDetected) {
  380         status = 'live'
  381       } else if (trustScore < 3 && !keywordDetected) {
  382         status = 'pending_review'  // New user queue
  383       } else if (keywordDetected) {
  384         status = 'pending_review'  // Keyword flagged
  385       }
  386
  387       // Insert gig
  388       const { data, error } = await db.from('gigs').insert({
  389         requester_id: currentUser.id,
  390         title: title,
  391         description: description,
  392         reward_amount: reward,
  393         location: location,
  394         expires_at: expires,
  395         status: status,
  396         auto_post: hasAutoPost
  397       }).select()
  398
  399       btn.disabled = false
  400       btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fa-solid fa-paper-plane"></i> Submit Gig'
  401
  402       if (error) {
  403         showError('Error submitting gig: ' + error.message)
  404         return
  405       }
  406
  407       // Show success
  408       const successMsg = document.getElementById('successMsg')
  409       const statusText = document.getElementById('submissionStatus')
  410
  411       if (status === 'live') {
  412         statusText.textContent = 'Your gig is now live and visible to Taskers!'
  413       } else {
  414         statusText.textContent = 'Your gig is pending admin review. You will be notified once approved.'
  415       }
  416
  417       successMsg.style.display = 'block'
  418       document.getElementById('gigForm').reset()
  419       document.getElementById('charCount').textContent = '0'
  420       document.getElementById('keywordWarning').style.display = 'none'
  421
  422       // Redirect after 3 seconds
  423       setTimeout(() => {
  424         window.location.href = 'live-gigs.html'
  425       }, 3000)
  426     })
  427
  428     function showError(msg) {
  429       const el = document.getElementById('errorMsg')
  430       el.textContent = '❌ ' + msg
  431       el.style.display = 'block'
  432       setTimeout(() => {
  433         el.style.display = 'none'
  434       }, 5000)
  435     }
  436
  437     async function doLogout() {
  438       const { error } = await db.auth.signOut()
  439       if (error) console.error('Logout error:', error)
  440       window.location.replace('index.html?logged=out')
  441     }
  442   </script>

● iTa'awun Development Session Summary

  Vision Document Overview (from iTaawun_Documentation.docx)

  Product: iTa'awun (نواعتلا - Mutual Assistance) - A student-centric physical freelance hub platform for Malaysian university students.

  Core Concepts:
  - Live Gigs - P2P task board where Members post micro-tasks, Taskers fulfill them
  - Campus Vendors - Shopee-style storefront for student products/services
  - Tiered Roles - Member → Tasker (admin-approved) → Asnaf (income-verified, hidden flag)
  - Trust Architecture - Trust score, keyword filters, photo proof, audit logs
  - 0% Commission - P2P direct payment, platform takes no cut

  ---
  Gap Analysis Completed

  ┌────────────────────────────────────┬─────────────┐
  │              Feature               │   Status    │
  ├────────────────────────────────────┼─────────────┤
  │ Basic auth (email)                 │ ✅ Existing │
  ├────────────────────────────────────┼─────────────┤
  │ Profiles (student/vendor/admin)    │ ✅ Existing │
  ├────────────────────────────────────┼─────────────┤
  │ Services table                     │ ✅ Existing │
  ├────────────────────────────────────┼─────────────┤
  │ Campus Vendors orders              │ ✅ Existing │
  ├────────────────────────────────────┼─────────────┤
  │ Admin dashboard                    │ ✅ Existing │
  ├────────────────────────────────────┼─────────────┤
  │ Live Gigs with Grab workflow       │ ❌ Missing  │
  ├────────────────────────────────────┼─────────────┤
  │ Tasker role + approval             │ ❌ Missing  │
  ├────────────────────────────────────┼─────────────┤
  │ Trust score system                 │ ❌ Missing  │
  ├────────────────────────────────────┼─────────────┤
  │ Academic integrity keyword filter  │ ❌ Missing  │
  ├────────────────────────────────────┼─────────────┤
  │ Photo proof completion             │ ❌ Missing  │
  ├────────────────────────────────────┼─────────────┤
  │ Asnaf verification + audit trail   │ ❌ Missing  │
  ├────────────────────────────────────┼─────────────┤
  │ Impact Report export               │ ❌ Missing  │
  ├────────────────────────────────────┼─────────────┤
  │ Community flagging (auto-hide @ 3) │ ❌ Missing  │
  └────────────────────────────────────┴─────────────┘

  ---
  Changes Made This Session

  1. Database Schema Updates (schema-updates.sql)

  Created comprehensive SQL migration adding:

  New Tables:
  - gigs - Live Gig posts with status workflow
  - gig_claims - Tasker claims (one per gig)
  - gig_completions - Photo proof + requester confirmation
  - gig_flags - Community reports (auto-hide at 3)
  - verifications - Asnaf income doc verification
  - audit_logs - Immutable action trail for authorities
  - keyword_filters - Banned academic integrity keywords

  New Columns on profiles:
  - trust_score - Increments on completions
  - is_asnaf - Hidden flag (admin-only visible)
  - matric_card_url - Optional trust badge
  - income_doc_url - Asnaf verification doc

  New Columns on services:
  - flag_count - Community reports
  - auto_post - Trust privilege (≥3 completions)
  - expires_at - Auto-expire old gigs

  Functions & Triggers:
  - check_gig_integrity() - Regex keyword scanner

  297     const SUPABASE_URL = 'https://fyahebgkacjsxmiwteny.supabase.co'
  298     const SUPABASE_KEY = 'eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9.eyJpc3MiOiJzdXBhYmFzZSIsInJlZiI6ImZ5YWhlYmdrYWNqc3htaXd0ZW55Iiwicm9s
      ZSI6ImFub24iLCJpYXQiOjE3NzAyNTg3NDEsImV4cCI6MjA4NTgzNDc0MX0.eIAWIPzB6EjW7rPKHLSsc2ryUBQ7yicRK1I-SxXg_2Y'
  299     const db = supabase.createClient(SUPABASE_URL, SUPABASE_KEY)
  300
  301     const BANNED_KEYWORDS = [
  302       'assignment', 'homework', 'exam', 'quiz', 'thesis', 'essay',
  303       'dissertation', 'paper', 'coursework', 'term paper', 'final project',
  304       'tugasan', 'ujian', 'tesis', 'karangan'
  305     ]
  306
  307     let currentUser = null
  308     let currentProfile = null
  309     let keywordDetected = false
  310
  311     // Auth check
  312     (async function init() {
  313       const { data: { session } } = await db.auth.getSession()
  314       if (!session) {
  315         window.location.href = 'index.html'
  316         return
  317       }
  318       currentUser = session.user
  319
  320       // Load profile
  321       const { data: profile } = await db.from('profiles').select('*').eq('id', currentUser.id).single()
  322       currentProfile = profile
  323
  324       if (profile?.avatar_url) {
  325         document.getElementById('profilePic').src = profile.avatar_url
  326       }
  327     })()
  328
  329     // Character count
  330     document.getElementById('description').addEventListener('input', function() {
  331       document.getElementById('charCount').textContent = this.value.length
  332     })
  333
  334     // Keyword detection
  335     function checkKeywords() {
  336       const title = document.getElementById('title').value.toLowerCase()
  337       const desc = document.getElementById('description').value.toLowerCase()
  338       const combined = title + ' ' + desc
  339
  340       keywordDetected = BANNED_KEYWORDS.some(keyword => {
  341         const regex = new RegExp('\\b' + keyword + '\\b', 'i')
  342         return regex.test(combined)
  343       })
  344
  345       const warning = document.getElementById('keywordWarning')
  346       warning.style.display = keywordDetected ? 'block' : 'none'
  347     }
  348
  349     // Form submission
  350     document.getElementById('gigForm').addEventListener('submit', async function(e) {
  351       e.preventDefault()
  352
  353       const title = document.getElementById('title').value.trim()
  354       const description = document.getElementById('description').value.trim()
  355       const reward = parseFloat(document.getElementById('reward').value)
  356       const location = document.getElementById('location').value.trim()
  357       const expires = document.getElementById('expires').value || null
  358
  359       if (!title || !description || !reward || !location) {
  360         showError('Please fill in all required fields.')
  361         return
  362       }
  363
  364       if (description.length > 500) {
  365         showError('Description must be 500 characters or less.')
  366         return
  367       }
  368
  369       const btn = document.getElementById('submitBtn')
  370       btn.disabled = true
  371       btn.textContent = 'Submitting...'
  372
  373       // Determine status based on trust score and keywords
  374       let status = 'pending_review'
  375       const trustScore = currentProfile?.trust_score || 0
  376       const hasAutoPost = currentProfile?.auto_post || false
  377
  378       // Auto-post if: trust score >= 3 AND no keywords detected
  379       if (trustScore >= 3 && !keywordDetected) {
  380         status = 'live'
  381       } else if (trustScore < 3 && !keywordDetected) {
  382         status = 'pending_review'  // New user queue
  383       } else if (keywordDetected) {
  384         status = 'pending_review'  // Keyword flagged
  385       }
  386
  387       // Insert gig
  388       const { data, error } = await db.from('gigs').insert({
  389         requester_id: currentUser.id,
  390         title: title,
  391         description: description,
  392         reward_amount: reward,
  393         location: location,
  394         expires_at: expires,
  395         status: status,
  396         auto_post: hasAutoPost
  397       }).select()
  398
  399       btn.disabled = false
  400       btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fa-solid fa-paper-plane"></i> Submit Gig'
  401
  402       if (error) {
  403         showError('Error submitting gig: ' + error.message)
  404         return
  405       }
  406
  407       // Show success
  408       const successMsg = document.getElementById('successMsg')
  409       const statusText = document.getElementById('submissionStatus')
  410
  411       if (status === 'live') {
  412         statusText.textContent = 'Your gig is now live and visible to Taskers!'
  413       } else {
  414         statusText.textContent = 'Your gig is pending admin review. You will be notified once approved.'
  415       }
  416
  417       successMsg.style.display = 'block'
  418       document.getElementById('gigForm').reset()
  419       document.getElementById('charCount').textContent = '0'
  420       document.getElementById('keywordWarning').style.display = 'none'
  421
  422       // Redirect after 3 seconds
  423       setTimeout(() => {
  424         window.location.href = 'live-gigs.html'
  425       }, 3000)
  426     })
  427
  428     function showError(msg) {
  429       const el = document.getElementById('errorMsg')
  430       el.textContent = '❌ ' + msg
  431       el.style.display = 'block'
  432       setTimeout(() => {
  433         el.style.display = 'none'
  434       }, 5000)
  435     }
  436
  437     async function doLogout() {
  438       const { error } = await db.auth.signOut()
  439       if (error) console.error('Logout error:', error)
  440       window.location.replace('index.html?logged=out')
  441     }

● iTa'awun Development Session Summary

  Vision Document Overview (from iTaawun_Documentation.docx)

  Product: iTa'awun (نواعتلا - Mutual Assistance) - A student-centric physical freelance hub platform for Malaysian university students.

  Core Concepts:
  - Live Gigs - P2P task board where Members post micro-tasks, Taskers fulfill them
  - Campus Vendors - Shopee-style storefront for student products/services
  - Tiered Roles - Member → Tasker (admin-approved) → Asnaf (income-verified, hidden flag)
  - Trust Architecture - Trust score, keyword filters, photo proof, audit logs
  - 0% Commission - P2P direct payment, platform takes no cut

  ---
  Gap Analysis Completed

  ---
  Changes Made This Session

  1. Database Schema Updates (schema-updates.sql)

  Created comprehensive SQL migration adding:

  New Tables:
  - gigs - Live Gig posts with status workflow
  - gig_claims - Tasker claims (one per gig)
  - gig_completions - Photo proof + requester confirmation
  - gig_flags - Community reports (auto-hide at 3)
  - verifications - Asnaf income doc verification
  - audit_logs - Immutable action trail for authorities
  - keyword_filters - Banned academic integrity keywords

  New Columns on profiles:
  - trust_score - Increments on completions
  - is_asnaf - Hidden flag (admin-only visible)
  - matric_card_url - Optional trust badge
  - income_doc_url - Asnaf verification doc

  New Columns on services:
  - flag_count - Community reports
  - auto_post - Trust privilege (≥3 completions)
  - expires_at - Auto-expire old gigs

  Functions & Triggers:
  - check_gig_integrity() - Regex keyword scanner
  - increment_trust_score() - Trust builder
  - check_gig_flags() - Auto-flag trigger @ 3 reports
  - log_audit() - Append-only audit logging

  326   <script>
  327     const SUPABASE_URL = 'https://fyahebgkacjsxmiwteny.supabase.co'
  328     const SUPABASE_KEY = 'eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9.eyJpc3MiOiJzdXBhYmFzZSIsInJlZiI6ImZ5YWhlYmdrYWNqc3htaXd0ZW55Iiwicm9s
      ZSI6ImFub24iLCJpYXQiOjE3NzAyNTg3NDEsImV4cCI6MjA4NTgzNDc0MX0.eIAWIPzB6EjW7rPKHLSsc2ryUBQ7yicRK1I-SxXg_2Y'
  329     const db = supabase.createClient(SUPABASE_URL, SUPABASE_KEY)
  330
  331     let currentUser = null
  332     let currentProfile = null
  333     let selectedFile = null
  334
  335     (async function init() {
  336       const { data: { session } } = await db.auth.getSession()
  337       if (!session) {
  338         window.location.href = 'index.html'
  339         return
  340       }
  341       currentUser = session.user
  342
  343       const { data: profile } = await db.from('profiles').select('*').eq('id', currentUser.id).single()
  344       currentProfile = profile
  345
  346       // Check application status
  347       if (profile?.role === 'tasker') {
  348         // Already approved
  349         document.getElementById('applicationSection').style.display = 'none'
  350         document.getElementById('approvedSection').style.display = 'block'
  351         document.getElementById('trustScoreDisplay').textContent = profile.trust_score || 0
  352         updateMilestoneText(profile.trust_score || 0)
  353       } else {
  354         // Check for pending application (stored in metadata or separate table)
  355         const { data: application } = await db.from('tasker_applications').select('*').eq('user_id', currentUser.id).eq('status', '
      pending').single()
  356
  357         if (application) {
  358           document.getElementById('applicationSection').style.display = 'none'
  359           document.getElementById('pendingSection').style.display = 'block'
  360         }
  361       }
  362     })()
  363
  364     function updateMilestoneText(score) {
  365       const el = document.getElementById('milestoneText')
  366       if (score >= 3) {
  367         el.textContent = '✓ Auto-post privilege unlocked!'
  368       } else {
  369         el.textContent = `Complete ${3 - score} more gigs to unlock auto-post privilege!`
  370       }
  371     }
  372
  373     function handleFileSelect() {
  374       const file = document.getElementById('matricFile').files[0]
  375       if (file) {
  376         selectedFile = file
  377         document.getElementById('matricFileName').textContent = '✓ Selected: ' + file.name
  378       }
  379     }
  380
  381     document.getElementById('taskerForm').addEventListener('submit', async function(e) {
  382       e.preventDefault()
  383
  384       const reason = document.getElementById('reason').value.trim()
  385       if (!reason) {
  386         alert('Please provide a reason for your application.')
  387         return
  388       }
  389
  390       const btn = document.getElementById('submitBtn')
  391       btn.disabled = true
  392       btn.textContent = 'Submitting...'
  393
  394       // For prototype: just update profile with pending flag
  395       // In production: upload matric card to storage, create application record
  396       const { error } = await db.from('profiles').update({
  397         role: 'tasker_pending',
  398         matric_card_url: selectedFile ? 'pending_upload' : null
  399       }).eq('id', currentUser.id)
  400
  401       // Create application record
  402       if (!error) {
  403         await db.from('tasker_applications').insert({
  404           user_id: currentUser.id,
  405           reason: reason,
  406           status: 'pending'
  407         })
  408       }
  409
  410       btn.disabled = false
  411       btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fa-solid fa-paper-plane"></i> Submit Application'
  412
  413       if (error) {
  414         alert('Error submitting application: ' + error.message)
  415         return
  416       }
  417
  418       document.getElementById('applicationSection').style.display = 'none'
  419       document.getElementById('pendingSection').style.display = 'block'
  420     })
  421
  422     async function doLogout() {
  423       const { error } = await db.auth.signOut()
  424       if (error) console.error('Logout error:', error)
  425       window.location.replace('index.html?logged=out')
  426     }

● iTa'awun Development Session Summary

  Vision Document Overview (from iTaawun_Documentation.docx)

  Product: iTa'awun (نواعتلا - Mutual Assistance) - A student-centric physical freelance hub platform for Malaysian university students.

  Core Concepts:
  - Live Gigs - P2P task board where Members post micro-tasks, Taskers fulfill them
  - Campus Vendors - Shopee-style storefront for student products/services
  - Tiered Roles - Member → Tasker (admin-approved) → Asnaf (income-verified, hidden flag)
  - Trust Architecture - Trust score, keyword filters, photo proof, audit logs
  - 0% Commission - P2P direct payment, platform takes no cut

  ---
  Gap Analysis Completed

  1. Database Schema Updates (schema-updates.sql)

  327     const SUPABASE_URL = 'https://fyahebgkacjsxmiwteny.supabase.co'
  328     const SUPABASE_KEY = 'eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9.eyJpc3MiOiJzdXBhYmFzZSIsInJlZiI6ImZ5YWhlYmdrYWNqc3htaXd0ZW55Iiwicm9s
      ZSI6ImFub24iLCJpYXQiOjE3NzAyNTg3NDEsImV4cCI6MjA4NTgzNDc0MX0.eIAWIPzB6EjW7rPKHLSsc2ryUBQ7yicRK1I-SxXg_2Y'
  329     const db = supabase.createClient(SUPABASE_URL, SUPABASE_KEY)
  330
  331     let currentUser = null
  332     let currentProfile = null
  333     let selectedFile = null
  334
  335     (async function init() {
  336       const { data: { session } } = await db.auth.getSession()
  337       if (!session) {
  338         window.location.href = 'index.html'
  339         return
  340       }
  341       currentUser = session.user
  342
  343       const { data: profile } = await db.from('profiles').select('*').eq('id', currentUser.id).single()
  344       currentProfile = profile
  345
  346       // Check application status
  347       if (profile?.role === 'tasker') {
  348         // Already approved
  349         document.getElementById('applicationSection').style.display = 'none'
  350         document.getElementById('approvedSection').style.display = 'block'
  351         document.getElementById('trustScoreDisplay').textContent = profile.trust_score || 0
  352         updateMilestoneText(profile.trust_score || 0)
  353       } else {
  354         // Check for pending application (stored in metadata or separate table)
  355         const { data: application } = await db.from('tasker_applications').select('*').eq('user_id', currentUser.id).eq('status', '
      pending').single()
  356
  357         if (application) {
  358           document.getElementById('applicationSection').style.display = 'none'
  359           document.getElementById('pendingSection').style.display = 'block'
  360         }
  361       }
  362     })()
  363
  364     function updateMilestoneText(score) {
  365       const el = document.getElementById('milestoneText')
  366       if (score >= 3) {
  367         el.textContent = '✓ Auto-post privilege unlocked!'
  368       } else {
  369         el.textContent = `Complete ${3 - score} more gigs to unlock auto-post privilege!`
  370       }
  371     }
  372
  373     function handleFileSelect() {
  374       const file = document.getElementById('matricFile').files[0]
  375       if (file) {
  376         selectedFile = file
  377         document.getElementById('matricFileName').textContent = '✓ Selected: ' + file.name
  378       }
  379     }
  380
  381     document.getElementById('taskerForm').addEventListener('submit', async function(e) {
  382       e.preventDefault()
  383
  384       const reason = document.getElementById('reason').value.trim()
  385       if (!reason) {
  386         alert('Please provide a reason for your application.')
  387         return
  388       }
  389
  390       const btn = document.getElementById('submitBtn')
  391       btn.disabled = true
  392       btn.textContent = 'Submitting...'
  393
  394       // For prototype: just update profile with pending flag
  395       // In production: upload matric card to storage, create application record
  396       const { error } = await db.from('profiles').update({
  397         role: 'tasker_pending',
  398         matric_card_url: selectedFile ? 'pending_upload' : null
  399       }).eq('id', currentUser.id)
  400
  401       // Create application record
  402       if (!error) {
  403         await db.from('tasker_applications').insert({
  404           user_id: currentUser.id,
  405           reason: reason,
  406           status: 'pending'
  407         })
  408       }
  409
  410       btn.disabled = false
  411       btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fa-solid fa-paper-plane"></i> Submit Application'
  412
  413       if (error) {
  414         alert('Error submitting application: ' + error.message)
  415         return
  416       }
  417
  418       document.getElementById('applicationSection').style.display = 'none'
  419       document.getElementById('pendingSection').style.display = 'block'
  420     })
  421
  422     async function doLogout() {
  423       const { error } = await db.auth.signOut()
  424       if (error) console.error('Logout error:', error)
  425       window.location.replace('index.html?logged=out')
  426     }

● iTa'awun Development Session Summary

  Vision Document Overview (from iTaawun_Documentation.docx)

  Product: iTa'awun (نواعتلا - Mutual Assistance) - A student-centric physical freelance hub platform for Malaysian university students.

  Core Concepts:
  - Live Gigs - P2P task board where Members post micro-tasks, Taskers fulfill them
  - Campus Vendors - Shopee-style storefront for student products/services
  - Tiered Roles - Member → Tasker (admin-approved) → Asnaf (income-verified, hidden flag)
  - Trust Architecture - Trust score, keyword filters, photo proof, audit logs
  - 0% Commission - P2P direct payment, platform takes no cut

  - audit_logs - Immutable action trail for authorities
  - keyword_filters - Banned academic integrity keywords

  New Columns on profiles:
  - trust_score - Increments on completions

  - income_doc_url - Asnaf verification doc

  New Columns on services:
  - flag_count - Community reports
  - auto_post - Trust privilege (≥3 completions)
  - expires_at - Auto-expire old gigs

  Functions & Triggers:
  - check_gig_integrity() - Regex keyword scanner
  - increment_trust_score() - Trust builder
  - check_gig_flags() - Auto-flag trigger @ 3 reports
  - log_audit() - Append-only audit logging

 Bash command

   cd "C:\Users\Iman Haqimi\Documents\Q\The Prodj\JV kutt\Codes\testitaawun" && echo "-- Tasker Applications Table (add to
   schema-updates.sql)

   CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS tasker_applications (
     id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
     user_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES auth.users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
     reason TEXT,
     matric_card_url TEXT,
     status VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'pending' CHECK (status IN ('pending', 'approved', 'rejected')),
     reviewed_by UUID REFERENCES auth.users(id),
     reviewed_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
     rejection_reason TEXT,
     created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()
   );

   CREATE INDEX idx_tasker_applications_user ON tasker_applications(user_id);
   CREATE INDEX idx_tasker_applications_status ON tasker_applications(status);

   ALTER TABLE tasker_applications ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;

   -- RLS Policies
   CREATE POLICY \"Users can read own applications\" ON tasker_applications
     FOR SELECT TO authenticated
     USING (auth.uid() = user_id);

   CREATE POLICY \"Users can create own applications\" ON tasker_applications
     FOR INSERT TO authenticated
     WITH CHECK (auth.uid() = user_id);

   CREATE POLICY \"Admins can read all applications\" ON tasker_applications
     FOR SELECT TO authenticated
     USING (
       EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM profiles p WHERE p.id = auth.uid() AND p.role = 'admin')
     );

   CREATE POLICY \"Admins can update applications\" ON tasker_applications
     FOR UPDATE TO authenticated
     USING (
       EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM profiles p WHERE p.id = auth.uid() AND p.role = 'admin')
     );
   " >> schema-updates.sql
   Append tasker_applications table to schema

● iTa'awun Development Session Summary

  Vision Document Overview (from iTaawun_Documentation.docx)

  Product: iTa'awun (نواعتلا - Mutual Assistance) - A student-centric physical freelance hub platform for Malaysian university students.

  Core Concepts:
  - Live Gigs - P2P task board where Members post micro-tasks, Taskers fulfill them
  - Campus Vendors - Shopee-style storefront for student products/services
  - Tiered Roles - Member → Tasker (admin-approved) → Asnaf (income-verified, hidden flag)
  - Trust Architecture - Trust score, keyword filters, photo proof, audit logs
  - 0% Commission - P2P direct payment, platform takes no cut

  ---
  Gap Analysis Completed

  Changes Made This Session

  1. Database Schema Updates (schema-updates.sql)

  Created comprehensive SQL migration adding:

  New Tables:
  - gigs - Live Gig posts with status workflow
  - gig_claims - Tasker claims (one per gig)
  - gig_completions - Photo proof + requester confirmation
  - gig_flags - Community reports (auto-hide at 3)
  - verifications - Asnaf income doc verification
  - audit_logs - Immutable action trail for authorities
  - keyword_filters - Banned academic integrity keywords

  New Columns on profiles:
  - trust_score - Increments on completions
  - is_asnaf - Hidden flag (admin-only visible)
  - matric_card_url - Optional trust badge
  - income_doc_url - Asnaf verification doc

  New Columns on services:
  - flag_count - Community reports
  - auto_post - Trust privilege (≥3 completions)
  - expires_at - Auto-expire old gigs

  Functions & Triggers:
  - check_gig_integrity() - Regex keyword scanner
  - increment_trust_score() - Trust builder
  - check_gig_flags() - Auto-flag trigger @ 3 reports
  - log_audit() - Append-only audit logging

────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 Bash command

   cd "C:\Users\Iman Haqimi\Documents\Q\The Prodj\JV kutt\Codes\testitaawun" && echo "-- Tasker Applications Table (add to
   schema-updates.sql)

   CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS tasker_applications (
     id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
     user_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES auth.users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
     reason TEXT,
     matric_card_url TEXT,
     status VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'pending' CHECK (status IN ('pending', 'approved', 'rejected')),
     reviewed_by UUID REFERENCES auth.users(id),
     reviewed_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
     rejection_reason TEXT,
     created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()
   );

   CREATE INDEX idx_tasker_applications_user ON tasker_applications(user_id);
   CREATE INDEX idx_tasker_applications_status ON tasker_applications(status);

   ALTER TABLE tasker_applications ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;

   -- RLS Policies
   CREATE POLICY \"Users can read own applications\" ON tasker_applications
     FOR SELECT TO authenticated
     USING (auth.uid() = user_id);

   CREATE POLICY \"Users can create own applications\" ON tasker_applications
     FOR INSERT TO authenticated
     WITH CHECK (auth.uid() = user_id);

   CREATE POLICY \"Admins can read all applications\" ON tasker_applications
     FOR SELECT TO authenticated
     USING (
       EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM profiles p WHERE p.id = auth.uid() AND p.role = 'admin')
     );

   CREATE POLICY \"Admins can update applications\" ON tasker_applications
     FOR UPDATE TO authenticated
     USING (
       EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM profiles p WHERE p.id = auth.uid() AND p.role = 'admin')
     );
   " >> schema-updates.sql
   Append tasker_applications table to schema

> Write a summary for the chats and changes here

● iTa'awun Development Session Summary

  Vision Document Overview (from iTaawun_Documentation.docx)

  Product: iTa'awun (نواعتلا - Mutual Assistance) - A student-centric physical freelance hub platform for Malaysian university students.

  Core Concepts:
  - Live Gigs - P2P task board where Members post micro-tasks, Taskers fulfill them
  - Campus Vendors - Shopee-style storefront for student products/services
  - Tiered Roles - Member → Tasker (admin-approved) → Asnaf (income-verified, hidden flag)
  - Trust Architecture - Trust score, keyword filters, photo proof, audit logs
  - 0% Commission - P2P direct payment, platform takes no cut

  Gap Analysis Completed

  ---
  Changes Made This Session

  1. Database Schema Updates (schema-updates.sql)

  Created comprehensive SQL migration adding:

  New Tables:
  - gigs - Live Gig posts with status workflow
  - gig_claims - Tasker claims (one per gig)
  - gig_completions - Photo proof + requester confirmation
  - gig_flags - Community reports (auto-hide at 3)
  - verifications - Asnaf income doc verification
  - audit_logs - Immutable action trail for authorities
  - keyword_filters - Banned academic integrity keywords

  New Columns on profiles:
  - trust_score - Increments on completions
  - is_asnaf - Hidden flag (admin-only visible)
  - matric_card_url - Optional trust badge
  - income_doc_url - Asnaf verification doc

  New Columns on services:
  - flag_count - Community reports
  - auto_post - Trust privilege (≥3 completions)
  - expires_at - Auto-expire old gigs

  Functions & Triggers:
  - check_gig_integrity() - Regex keyword scanner
  - increment_trust_score() - Trust builder
  - check_gig_flags() - Auto-flag trigger @ 3 reports
  - log_audit() - Append-only audit logging

  353     (async function init() {
  354       const { data: { session } } = await db.auth.getSession()
  355       if (!session) {
  356         window.location.href = 'index.html'
  357         return
  358       }
  359       currentUser = session.user
  360
  361       const { data: profile } = await db.from('profiles').select('avatar_url').eq('id', currentUser.id).single()
  362       if (profile?.avatar_url) {
  363         document.getElementById('profilePic').src = profile.avatar_url
  364       }
  365
  366       loadGigs()
  367     })()

  369     function switchTab(tab) {
  370       currentTab = tab
  371       document.querySelectorAll('.tab-btn').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'))
  372       event.target.classList.add('active')
  373       loadGigs()
  374     }
  375
  376     async function loadGigs() {
  377       const container = document.getElementById('gigsContainer')
  378       container.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state"><i class="fa-solid fa-spinner fa-spin"></i><p>Loading...</p></div>'
  379
  380       if (currentTab === 'posted') {
  381         // Gigs I posted
  382         const { data: gigs } = await db.from('gigs').select(`
  383           *,
  384           claim:gig_claims(tasker_id, tasker:profiles(full_name, avatar_url)),
  385           completion:gig_completions(proof_photo_url, submitted_at, confirmed_by_requester, dispute_raised)
  386         `).eq('requester_id', currentUser.id).order('created_at', { ascending: false })
  387
  388         if (!gigs || gigs.length === 0) {
  389           container.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state"><i class="fa-solid fa-clipboard-list"></i><p>You haven\'t posted any gigs
       yet.</p><button class="btn btn-view" onclick="window.location.href=\'post-gig.html\'" style="margin-top:15px">Post Your First Gig<
      /button></div>'
  390           return
  391         }
  392
  393         container.innerHTML = gigs.map(gig => renderPostedGig(gig)).join('')
  394       } else {
  395         // Gigs I claimed
  396         const { data: claims } = await db.from('gig_claims').select(`
  397           *,
  398           gig:gigs(title, description, reward_amount, location, requester_id, requester:profiles(full_name, avatar_url)),
  399           completion:gig_completions(id, proof_photo_url, confirmed_by_requester, dispute_raised)
  400         `).eq('tasker_id', currentUser.id).order('claimed_at', { ascending: false })
  401
  402         if (!claims || claims.length === 0) {
  403           container.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state"><i class="fa-solid fa-hand-holding-hand"></i><p>You haven\'t claimed any
      gigs yet.</p><button class="btn btn-view" onclick="window.location.href=\'live-gigs.html\'" style="margin-top:15px">Browse Live Gig
      s</button></div>'
  404           return
  405         }
  406
  407         container.innerHTML = claims.map(claim => renderClaimedGig(claim)).join('')
  408       }
  409     }
  410
  411     function renderPostedGig(gig) {
  412       const claim = gig.claim?.[0]
  413       const tasker = claim?.tasker
  414       const completion = gig.completion?.[0]
  415       const reward = parseFloat(gig.reward_amount || 0).toFixed(2)
  416
  417       let actionSection = ''
  418       if (gig.status === 'pending_review') {
  419         actionSection = '<button class="btn btn-view" disabled>⏳ Pending Review</button>'
  420       } else if (gig.status === 'live') {
  421         actionSection = '<button class="btn btn-view" disabled>🟢 Live - Waiting for Tasker</button>'
  422       } else if (gig.status === 'grabbed' && claim) {
  423         actionSection = `
  424           <div class="tasker-info">
  425             <img src="${tasker.avatar_url || 'assets/images/OIP.jpg'}" class="tasker-avatar">
  426             <span><strong>${escapeHtml(tasker.full_name)}</strong> is working on this</span>
  427           </div>
  428           <button class="btn btn-view" onclick="viewClaimedGig('${gig.id}')">View Progress</button>
  429         `
  430       } else if (gig.status === 'completed') {
  431         actionSection = '<button class="btn btn-view" disabled>✓ Completed</button>'
  432       } else if (gig.status === 'flagged') {
  433         actionSection = '<button class="btn btn-view" disabled>⚠️ Flagged for Review</button>'
  434       }
  435
  436       return `
  437         <div class="gig-card">
  438           <div class="gig-header">
  439             <h3 class="gig-title">${escapeHtml(gig.title)}</h3>
  440             <div class="gig-meta">
  441               <span class="status-badge status-${gig.status}">${gig.status.replace('_', ' ')}</span>
  442               <span class="gig-reward">RM${reward}</span>
  443             </div>
  444           </div>
  445           <div class="gig-body">
  446             <p class="gig-desc">${escapeHtml(gig.description)}</p>
  447             <p class="gig-location"><i class="fa-solid fa-location-dot"></i> ${escapeHtml(gig.location)}</p>
  448           </div>
  449           <div class="gig-footer">
  450             ${actionSection}
  451             ${(gig.status === 'live' || gig.status === 'pending_review') ? `<button class="btn btn-delete" onclick="deleteGig('${gi
      g.id}')" style="margin-top:8px;width:100%">Delete Gig</button>` : ''}
  452           </div>
  453         </div>
  454       `
  455     }
  456
  457     function renderClaimedGig(claim) {
  458       const gig = claim.gig
  459       const completion = claim.completion?.[0]
  460       const reward = parseFloat(gig.reward_amount || 0).toFixed(2)
  461
  462       let actionSection = ''
  463       if (completion) {
  464         if (completion.dispute_raised) {
  465           actionSection = '<button class="btn btn-dispute" disabled>⚠️ Dispute Raised</button>'
  466         } else if (completion.confirmed_by_requester) {
  467           actionSection = '<button class="btn btn-confirm" disabled>✓ Confirmed by Requester</button>'
  468         } else {
  469           actionSection = '<button class="btn btn-view" disabled>⏳ Awaiting Confirmation</button>'
  470         }
  471       } else {
  472         actionSection = `<button class="btn btn-confirm" onclick="openProofModal('${claim.id}')">📸 Submit Proof</button>`
  473       }
  474
  475       return `
  476         <div class="gig-card">
  477           <div class="gig-header">
  478             <h3 class="gig-title">${escapeHtml(gig.title)}</h3>
  479             <div class="gig-meta">
  480               <span class="status-badge status-${gig.status || 'grabbed'}">${(gig.status || 'grabbed').replace('_', ' ')}</span>
  481               <span class="gig-reward">RM${reward}</span>
  482             </div>
  483           </div>
  484           <div class="gig-body">
  485             <p class="gig-desc">${escapeHtml(gig.description)}</p>
  486             <p class="gig-location"><i class="fa-solid fa-location-dot"></i> ${escapeHtml(gig.location)}</p>
  487             <p style="font-size:12px;color:#999"><i class="fa-solid fa-user"></i> Requester: ${escapeHtml(gig.requester?.full_name
      || 'Anonymous')}</p>
  488           </div>
  489           <div class="gig-footer">
  490             ${actionSection}
  491           </div>
  492         </div>
  493       `
  494     }
  495
  496     function escapeHtml(text) {
  497       if (!text) return ''
  498       return String(text).replace(/&/g, '&amp;').replace(/</g, '&lt;').replace(/>/g, '&gt;').replace(/"/g, '&quot;')
  499     }

  502     function openProofModal(claimId) {
  503       selectedClaimId = claimId
  504       selectedProofFile = null
  505       document.getElementById('proofFileName').textContent = ''
  506       document.getElementById('proofModal').style.display = 'block'
  507     }
  508
  509     function closeProofModal() {
  510       document.getElementById('proofModal').style.display = 'none'
  511     }

  513     function handleProofSelect() {
  514       selectedProofFile = document.getElementById('proofFile').files[0]
  515       if (selectedProofFile) {
  516         document.getElementById('proofFileName').textContent = '✓ ' + selectedProofFile.name
  517       }
  518     }
  519
  520     async function submitProof() {
  521       if (!selectedClaimId || !selectedProofFile) {
  522         alert('Please select a photo first.')
  523         return
  524       }
  525
  526       // For prototype: store as data URL (in production, upload to Supabase Storage)
  527       const reader = new FileReader()
  528       reader.onload = async function(e) {
  529         const photoUrl = e.target.result // In prod: upload to storage and get URL
  530
  531         const { error } = await db.from('gig_completions').insert({
  532           claim_id: selectedClaimId,
  533           proof_photo_url: 'prototype_placeholder.jpg' // Replace with actual storage URL
  534         })
  535
  536         if (error) {
  537           alert('Error submitting proof: ' + error.message)
  538           return
  539         }
  540
  541         closeProofModal()
  542         alert('✅ Proof submitted! Requester will review and confirm.')
  543         loadGigs()
  544       }
  545       reader.readAsDataURL(selectedProofFile)
  546     }
  547
  548     // Dispute
  549     function openDisputeModal(claimId) {
  550       selectedClaimId = claimId
  551       document.getElementById('disputeReason').value = ''
  552       document.getElementById('disputeModal').style.display = 'block'
  553     }
  554
  555     function closeDisputeModal() {
  556       document.getElementById('disputeModal').style.display = 'none'
  557     }
  558
  559     async function submitDispute() {
  560       const reason = document.getElementById('disputeReason').value.trim()
  561       if (!reason) {
  562         alert('Please provide a reason for the dispute.')
  563         return
  564       }
  565
  566       const { error } = await db.from('gig_completions').update({
  567         dispute_raised: true
  568       }).eq('claim_id', selectedClaimId)
  569
  570       if (error) {
  571         alert('Error raising dispute: ' + error.message)
  572         return
  573       }
  574
  575       closeDisputeModal()
  576       alert('⚠️ Dispute raised. Admin will review and arbitrate.')
  577       loadGigs()
  578     }
  579
  580     async function deleteGig(gigId) {
  581       if (!confirm('Delete this gig? This cannot be undone.')) return
  582
  583       const { error } = await db.from('gigs').delete().eq('id', gigId)
  584       if (error) {
  585         alert('Error deleting gig: ' + error.message)
  586         return
  587       }
  588
  589       loadGigs()
  590     }
  591
  592     async function doLogout() {
  593       const { error } = await db.auth.signOut()
  594       if (error) console.error('Logout error:', error)
  595       window.location.replace('index.html?logged=out')
  596     }

> Write a summary for the chats and changes here

● iTa'awun Development Session Summary

  Vision Document Overview (from iTaawun_Documentation.docx)

  Product: iTa'awun (نواعتلا - Mutual Assistance) - A student-centric physical freelance hub platform for Malaysian university students.

  Core Concepts:
  - Live Gigs - P2P task board where Members post micro-tasks, Taskers fulfill them
  - Campus Vendors - Shopee-style storefront for student products/services
  - Tiered Roles - Member → Tasker (admin-approved) → Asnaf (income-verified, hidden flag)
  - Trust Architecture - Trust score, keyword filters, photo proof, audit logs
  - 0% Commission - P2P direct payment, platform takes no cut

  ---
  Gap Analysis Completed

  ┌────────────────────────────────────┬─────────────┐

  └────────────────────────────────────┴─────────────┘

  ---
  Changes Made This Session

  1. Database Schema Updates (schema-updates.sql)

  Created comprehensive SQL migration adding:

  New Tables:
  - gigs - Live Gig posts with status workflow
  - gig_claims - Tasker claims (one per gig)
  - gig_completions - Photo proof + requester confirmation
  - gig_flags - Community reports (auto-hide at 3)
  - verifications - Asnaf income doc verification
  - audit_logs - Immutable action trail for authorities
  - keyword_filters - Banned academic integrity keywords

  New Columns on profiles:
  - trust_score - Increments on completions
  - is_asnaf - Hidden flag (admin-only visible)
  - matric_card_url - Optional trust badge
  - income_doc_url - Asnaf verification doc

  New Columns on services:
  - flag_count - Community reports
  - auto_post - Trust privilege (≥3 completions)
  - expires_at - Auto-expire old gigs

  Functions & Triggers:
  - check_gig_integrity() - Regex keyword scanner
  - increment_trust_score() - Trust builder
  - check_gig_flags() - Auto-flag trigger @ 3 reports
  - log_audit() - Append-only audit logging

  ---

  Files to Create/Update:

  348     let currentUser = null
  349     let currentTab = 'posted'
  350     let selectedClaimId = null

  353     (async function init() {
  354       const { data: { session } } = await db.auth.getSession()
  355       if (!session) {
  356         window.location.href = 'index.html'
  357         return
  358       }
  359       currentUser = session.user
  360
  361       const { data: profile } = await db.from('profiles').select('avatar_url').eq('id', currentUser.id).single()
  362       if (profile?.avatar_url) {
  363         document.getElementById('profilePic').src = profile.avatar_url
  364       }
  365
  366       loadGigs()
  367     })()

  369     function switchTab(tab) {
  370       currentTab = tab
  371       document.querySelectorAll('.tab-btn').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'))
  372       event.target.classList.add('active')
  373       loadGigs()
  374     }
  375
  376     async function loadGigs() {
  377       const container = document.getElementById('gigsContainer')
  378       container.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state"><i class="fa-solid fa-spinner fa-spin"></i><p>Loading...</p></div>'
  379
  380       if (currentTab === 'posted') {
  381         // Gigs I posted
  382         const { data: gigs } = await db.from('gigs').select(`
  383           *,
  384           claim:gig_claims(tasker_id, tasker:profiles(full_name, avatar_url)),
  385           completion:gig_completions(proof_photo_url, submitted_at, confirmed_by_requester, dispute_raised)
  386         `).eq('requester_id', currentUser.id).order('created_at', { ascending: false })
  387
  388         if (!gigs || gigs.length === 0) {
  389           container.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state"><i class="fa-solid fa-clipboard-list"></i><p>You haven\'t posted any gigs
       yet.</p><button class="btn btn-view" onclick="window.location.href=\'post-gig.html\'" style="margin-top:15px">Post Your First Gig<
      /button></div>'
  390           return
  391         }
  392
  393         container.innerHTML = gigs.map(gig => renderPostedGig(gig)).join('')
  394       } else {
  395         // Gigs I claimed
  396         const { data: claims } = await db.from('gig_claims').select(`
  397           *,
  398           gig:gigs(title, description, reward_amount, location, requester_id, requester:profiles(full_name, avatar_url)),
  399           completion:gig_completions(id, proof_photo_url, confirmed_by_requester, dispute_raised)
  400         `).eq('tasker_id', currentUser.id).order('claimed_at', { ascending: false })
  401
  402         if (!claims || claims.length === 0) {
  403           container.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state"><i class="fa-solid fa-hand-holding-hand"></i><p>You haven\'t claimed any
      gigs yet.</p><button class="btn btn-view" onclick="window.location.href=\'live-gigs.html\'" style="margin-top:15px">Browse Live Gig
      s</button></div>'
  404           return
  405         }
  406
  407         container.innerHTML = claims.map(claim => renderClaimedGig(claim)).join('')
  408       }
  409     }
  410
  411     function renderPostedGig(gig) {
  412       const claim = gig.claim?.[0]
  413       const tasker = claim?.tasker
  414       const completion = gig.completion?.[0]
  415       const reward = parseFloat(gig.reward_amount || 0).toFixed(2)
  416
  417       let actionSection = ''
  418       if (gig.status === 'pending_review') {
  419         actionSection = '<button class="btn btn-view" disabled>⏳ Pending Review</button>'
  420       } else if (gig.status === 'live') {
  421         actionSection = '<button class="btn btn-view" disabled>🟢 Live - Waiting for Tasker</button>'
  422       } else if (gig.status === 'grabbed' && claim) {
  423         actionSection = `
  424           <div class="tasker-info">
  425             <img src="${tasker.avatar_url || 'assets/images/OIP.jpg'}" class="tasker-avatar">
  426             <span><strong>${escapeHtml(tasker.full_name)}</strong> is working on this</span>
  427           </div>
  428           <button class="btn btn-view" onclick="viewClaimedGig('${gig.id}')">View Progress</button>
  429         `
  430       } else if (gig.status === 'completed') {
  431         actionSection = '<button class="btn btn-view" disabled>✓ Completed</button>'
  432       } else if (gig.status === 'flagged') {
  433         actionSection = '<button class="btn btn-view" disabled>⚠️ Flagged for Review</button>'
  434       }
  435
  436       return `
  437         <div class="gig-card">
  438           <div class="gig-header">
  439             <h3 class="gig-title">${escapeHtml(gig.title)}</h3>
  440             <div class="gig-meta">
  441               <span class="status-badge status-${gig.status}">${gig.status.replace('_', ' ')}</span>
  442               <span class="gig-reward">RM${reward}</span>
  443             </div>
  444           </div>
  445           <div class="gig-body">
  446             <p class="gig-desc">${escapeHtml(gig.description)}</p>
  447             <p class="gig-location"><i class="fa-solid fa-location-dot"></i> ${escapeHtml(gig.location)}</p>
  448           </div>
  449           <div class="gig-footer">
  450             ${actionSection}
  451             ${(gig.status === 'live' || gig.status === 'pending_review') ? `<button class="btn btn-delete" onclick="deleteGig('${gi
      g.id}')" style="margin-top:8px;width:100%">Delete Gig</button>` : ''}
  452           </div>
  453         </div>
  454       `
  455     }
  456
  457     function renderClaimedGig(claim) {
  458       const gig = claim.gig
  459       const completion = claim.completion?.[0]
  460       const reward = parseFloat(gig.reward_amount || 0).toFixed(2)
  461
  462       let actionSection = ''
  463       if (completion) {
  464         if (completion.dispute_raised) {
  465           actionSection = '<button class="btn btn-dispute" disabled>⚠️ Dispute Raised</button>'
  466         } else if (completion.confirmed_by_requester) {
  467           actionSection = '<button class="btn btn-confirm" disabled>✓ Confirmed by Requester</button>'
  468         } else {
  469           actionSection = '<button class="btn btn-view" disabled>⏳ Awaiting Confirmation</button>'
  470         }
  471       } else {
  472         actionSection = `<button class="btn btn-confirm" onclick="openProofModal('${claim.id}')">📸 Submit Proof</button>`
  473       }
  474
  475       return `
  476         <div class="gig-card">
  477           <div class="gig-header">
  478             <h3 class="gig-title">${escapeHtml(gig.title)}</h3>
  479             <div class="gig-meta">
  480               <span class="status-badge status-${gig.status || 'grabbed'}">${(gig.status || 'grabbed').replace('_', ' ')}</span>
  481               <span class="gig-reward">RM${reward}</span>
  482             </div>
  483           </div>
  484           <div class="gig-body">
  485             <p class="gig-desc">${escapeHtml(gig.description)}</p>
  486             <p class="gig-location"><i class="fa-solid fa-location-dot"></i> ${escapeHtml(gig.location)}</p>
  487             <p style="font-size:12px;color:#999"><i class="fa-solid fa-user"></i> Requester: ${escapeHtml(gig.requester?.full_name
      || 'Anonymous')}</p>
  488           </div>
  489           <div class="gig-footer">
  490             ${actionSection}
  491           </div>
  492         </div>
  493       `
  494     }
  495
  496     function escapeHtml(text) {
  497       if (!text) return ''
  498       return String(text).replace(/&/g, '&amp;').replace(/</g, '&lt;').replace(/>/g, '&gt;').replace(/"/g, '&quot;')
  499     }

  501     // Proof upload
  502     function openProofModal(claimId) {
  503       selectedClaimId = claimId
  504       selectedProofFile = null
  505       document.getElementById('proofFileName').textContent = ''
  506       document.getElementById('proofModal').style.display = 'block'
  507     }
  508
  509     function closeProofModal() {
  510       document.getElementById('proofModal').style.display = 'none'
  511     }

  513     function handleProofSelect() {
  514       selectedProofFile = document.getElementById('proofFile').files[0]
  515       if (selectedProofFile) {
  516         document.getElementById('proofFileName').textContent = '✓ ' + selectedProofFile.name
  517       }
  518     }
  519
  520     async function submitProof() {
  521       if (!selectedClaimId || !selectedProofFile) {
  522         alert('Please select a photo first.')
  523         return
  524       }
  525
  526       // For prototype: store as data URL (in production, upload to Supabase Storage)
  527       const reader = new FileReader()
  528       reader.onload = async function(e) {
  529         const photoUrl = e.target.result // In prod: upload to storage and get URL
  530
  531         const { error } = await db.from('gig_completions').insert({
  532           claim_id: selectedClaimId,
  533           proof_photo_url: 'prototype_placeholder.jpg' // Replace with actual storage URL
  534         })
  535
  536         if (error) {
  537           alert('Error submitting proof: ' + error.message)
  538           return
  539         }
  540
  541         closeProofModal()
  542         alert('✅ Proof submitted! Requester will review and confirm.')
  543         loadGigs()
  544       }
  545       reader.readAsDataURL(selectedProofFile)
  546     }
  547
  548     // Dispute
  549     function openDisputeModal(claimId) {
  550       selectedClaimId = claimId
  551       document.getElementById('disputeReason').value = ''
  552       document.getElementById('disputeModal').style.display = 'block'
  553     }
  554
  555     function closeDisputeModal() {
  556       document.getElementById('disputeModal').style.display = 'none'
  557     }
  558
  559     async function submitDispute() {
  560       const reason = document.getElementById('disputeReason').value.trim()
  561       if (!reason) {
  562         alert('Please provide a reason for the dispute.')
  563         return
  564       }
  565
  566       const { error } = await db.from('gig_completions').update({
  567         dispute_raised: true
  568       }).eq('claim_id', selectedClaimId)
  569
  570       if (error) {
  571         alert('Error raising dispute: ' + error.message)
  572         return
  573       }
  574
  575       closeDisputeModal()
  576       alert('⚠️ Dispute raised. Admin will review and arbitrate.')
  577       loadGigs()
  578     }
  579
  580     async function deleteGig(gigId) {
  581       if (!confirm('Delete this gig? This cannot be undone.')) return
  582
  583       const { error } = await db.from('gigs').delete().eq('id', gigId)
  584       if (error) {
  585         alert('Error deleting gig: ' + error.message)
  586         return
  587       }
  588
  589       loadGigs()
  590     }
  591
  592     async function doLogout() {
  593       const { error } = await db.auth.signOut()
  594       if (error) console.error('Logout error:', error)
  595       window.location.replace('index.html?logged=out')
  596     }

> Write a summary for the chats and changes here

● iTa'awun Development Session Summary

  Vision Document Overview (from iTaawun_Documentation.docx)

  Product: iTa'awun (نواعتلا - Mutual Assistance) - A student-centric physical freelance hub platform for Malaysian university students.

  Core Concepts:
  - Live Gigs - P2P task board where Members post micro-tasks, Taskers fulfill them
  - Campus Vendors - Shopee-style storefront for student products/services
  - Tiered Roles - Member → Tasker (admin-approved) → Asnaf (income-verified, hidden flag)
  - Trust Architecture - Trust score, keyword filters, photo proof, audit logs
  - 0% Commission - P2P direct payment, platform takes no cut

  ---
  Gap Analysis Completed

  ---
  Changes Made This Session

  1. Database Schema Updates (schema-updates.sql)

  Created comprehensive SQL migration adding:

  New Tables:
  - gigs - Live Gig posts with status workflow
  - gig_claims - Tasker claims (one per gig)
  - gig_completions - Photo proof + requester confirmation
  - gig_flags - Community reports (auto-hide at 3)
  - verifications - Asnaf income doc verification
  - audit_logs - Immutable action trail for authorities
  - keyword_filters - Banned academic integrity keywords

  New Columns on profiles:
  - trust_score - Increments on completions
  - is_asnaf - Hidden flag (admin-only visible)
  - matric_card_url - Optional trust badge
  - income_doc_url - Asnaf verification doc

  New Columns on services:
  - flag_count - Community reports
  - auto_post - Trust privilege (≥3 completions)
  - expires_at - Auto-expire old gigs

  Functions & Triggers:
  - check_gig_integrity() - Regex keyword scanner
  - increment_trust_score() - Trust builder
  - check_gig_flags() - Auto-flag trigger @ 3 reports
  - log_audit() - Append-only audit logging

● iTa'awun Development Session Summary

  Vision Document Overview (from iTaawun_Documentation.docx)

  Product: iTa'awun (نواعتلا - Mutual Assistance) - A student-centric physical freelance hub platform for Malaysian university students.

  Core Concepts:
  - Live Gigs - P2P task board where Members post micro-tasks, Taskers fulfill them
  - Campus Vendors - Shopee-style storefront for student products/services
  - Tiered Roles - Member → Tasker (admin-approved) → Asnaf (income-verified, hidden flag)
  - Trust Architecture - Trust score, keyword filters, photo proof, audit logs
  - 0% Commission - P2P direct payment, platform takes no cut

  ---
  Gap Analysis Completed

  ---
  Changes Made This Session

  1. Database Schema Updates (schema-updates.sql)

  Created comprehensive SQL migration adding:

  New Tables:
  - gigs - Live Gig posts with status workflow
  - gig_claims - Tasker claims (one per gig)
  - gig_completions - Photo proof + requester confirmation
  - gig_flags - Community reports (auto-hide at 3)
  - verifications - Asnaf income doc verification
  - audit_logs - Immutable action trail for authorities
  - keyword_filters - Banned academic integrity keywords

  New Columns on profiles:
  - trust_score - Increments on completions
  - is_asnaf - Hidden flag (admin-only visible)
  - matric_card_url - Optional trust badge
  - income_doc_url - Asnaf verification doc

  New Columns on services:
  - flag_count - Community reports
  - auto_post - Trust privilege (≥3 completions)
  - expires_at - Auto-expire old gigs

  Functions & Triggers:
  - check_gig_integrity() - Regex keyword scanner
  - increment_trust_score() - Trust builder
  - check_gig_flags() - Auto-flag trigger @ 3 reports
  - log_audit() - Append-only audit logging

> Write a summary for the chats and changes here

● iTa'awun Development Session Summary

  Vision Document Overview (from iTaawun_Documentation.docx)

  Product: iTa'awun (نواعتلا - Mutual Assistance) - A student-centric physical freelance hub platform for Malaysian university students.

  Core Concepts:
  - Live Gigs - P2P task board where Members post micro-tasks, Taskers fulfill them
  - Campus Vendors - Shopee-style storefront for student products/services
  - Tiered Roles - Member → Tasker (admin-approved) → Asnaf (income-verified, hidden flag)
  - Trust Architecture - Trust score, keyword filters, photo proof, audit logs
  - 0% Commission - P2P direct payment, platform takes no cut

  ---
  Gap Analysis Completed

  ┌────────────────────────────────────┬─────────────┐

  ---
  Changes Made This Session

  1. Database Schema Updates (schema-updates.sql)

  Created comprehensive SQL migration adding:

  New Tables:
  - gigs - Live Gig posts with status workflow
  - gig_claims - Tasker claims (one per gig)
  - gig_completions - Photo proof + requester confirmation
  - gig_flags - Community reports (auto-hide at 3)
  - verifications - Asnaf income doc verification
  - audit_logs - Immutable action trail for authorities
  - keyword_filters - Banned academic integrity keywords

  New Columns on profiles:
  - trust_score - Increments on completions
  - is_asnaf - Hidden flag (admin-only visible)
  - matric_card_url - Optional trust badge
  - income_doc_url - Asnaf verification doc

  New Columns on services:
  - flag_count - Community reports
  - auto_post - Trust privilege (≥3 completions)
  - expires_at - Auto-expire old gigs

  Functions & Triggers:
  - check_gig_integrity() - Regex keyword scanner
  - increment_trust_score() - Trust builder
  - check_gig_flags() - Auto-flag trigger @ 3 reports
  - log_audit() - Append-only audit logging

  ---

  Files to Create/Update:

● iTa'awun Development Session Summary

  Vision Document Overview (from iTaawun_Documentation.docx)

  Product: iTa'awun (نواعتلا - Mutual Assistance) - A student-centric physical freelance hub platform for Malaysian university students.

  Core Concepts:
  - Live Gigs - P2P task board where Members post micro-tasks, Taskers fulfill them
  - Campus Vendors - Shopee-style storefront for student products/services
  - Tiered Roles - Member → Tasker (admin-approved) → Asnaf (income-verified, hidden flag)
  - Trust Architecture - Trust score, keyword filters, photo proof, audit logs
  - 0% Commission - P2P direct payment, platform takes no cut

  ---
  Gap Analysis Completed

  Changes Made This Session

  1. Database Schema Updates (schema-updates.sql)

  Created comprehensive SQL migration adding:

  New Tables:
  - gigs - Live Gig posts with status workflow
  - gig_claims - Tasker claims (one per gig)
  - gig_completions - Photo proof + requester confirmation
  - gig_flags - Community reports (auto-hide at 3)
  - verifications - Asnaf income doc verification
  - audit_logs - Immutable action trail for authorities
  - keyword_filters - Banned academic integrity keywords

  New Columns on profiles:
  - trust_score - Increments on completions
  - is_asnaf - Hidden flag (admin-only visible)
  - matric_card_url - Optional trust badge
  - income_doc_url - Asnaf verification doc

  New Columns on services:
  - flag_count - Community reports
  - auto_post - Trust privilege (≥3 completions)
  - expires_at - Auto-expire old gigs

  Functions & Triggers:
  - check_gig_integrity() - Regex keyword scanner
  - increment_trust_score() - Trust builder
  - check_gig_flags() - Auto-flag trigger @ 3 reports
  - log_audit() - Append-only audit logging
